		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/092_forgot_password_admin/plugin.inc.php');

			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/092_forgot_password_admin/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}

		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/092_forgot_password_admin/plugin.inc.php') !== 'cd10252c79aec9a138a2c8bd8ac2c2356c0959a3') {
